n=5 example:
adj_list[0] = []  # empty if node 0 has no connections
adj_list[1] = [(3, 101, 1672541000, 1), (4, 102, 1672542000, 2)]  # node 1 connected to nodes 3 and 4
adj_list[2] = [(5, 103, 1672543000, 3)]  # node 2 connected to node 5
adj_list[3] = [(1, 101, 1672541000, 1)]  # node 3 connected to node 1
adj_list[4] = [(1, 102, 1672542000, 2)]  # node 4 connected to node 1


neighbor, edge, time, index
neighbor: ID of the connected node
edge: unique identifier for this connection
time: timestamp of when the interaction occurred
index: sequential index of the interaction in the dataset
